style="height:18pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div></div><div id="i326a37f695b84a82a759627cbe55294d_7"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:45pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div style="-sec-extract:summary;text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Item 5.04.             Temporary Suspension of Trading under Registrant's Employee Benefit Plans.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On November 23, 2021, 3M Company (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) sent a notice (the &#8220;Blackout Notice&#8221;) to its directors and executive officers informing them of a blackout period that will begin at 3:00 P.M. Central Time on December 27, 2021 and end the week of January 9, 2022 (the &#8220;Blackout Period&#8221;). The Blackout Period is being imposed to allow for the transfer of administrative records in connection with a change in record keepers for the 3M Voluntary Investment Plan and Employee Stock Ownership Plan and the 3M Savings Plan (the &#8220;Plans&#8221;). </span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">During the Blackout Period, participants in the Plans will have limited access to their accounts, and will be unable to check their account balances, transfer or diversify their investments or obtain a loan, withdrawal or distribution from their Plan accounts. The Blackout Notice informed the directors and executive officers that, during the Blackout Period, they will be prohibited from, directly or indirectly, purchasing, selling, or otherwise acquiring or transferring any equity security of the Company acquired in connection with their service as a director or employment as an officer.  </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">During the Blackout Period and for a period of two years after the ending date of the Blackout Period, the Company&#8217;s security holders and other interested persons may obtain, without charge, information regarding the Blackout Period, including the actual ending date of the Blackout Period, by contacting the Company&#8217;s Assistant Secretary at (651) 737-8503 or in writing at 3M Company, 3M Center, 220-10E-09, St. Paul, MN 55144.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">A copy of the Blackout Notice is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Item 9.01.  Financial Statements and Exhibits</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">(d) We are required to provide this notice to you under Rule 104 of Regulation BTR promulgated by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission pursuant to Section 306(a) of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Reason for the Blackout Period</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The blackout period is being imposed to allow for the transfer of administrative records in connection with a change in record keepers for the Plans to Empower Retirement.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Length of Blackout Period</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The blackout period will begin at 3&#58;00 P.M. Central Time on December 27, 2021 and will end the week of January 9, 2022.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Impact on Plan Participant Rights</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">During the Blackout Period, Plan participants will have limited access to their accounts, and will be unable to check their account balances, transfer or diversify their investments or obtain a loan, withdrawal or distribution from their Plan accounts.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Restrictions on Directors and Executive Officers During the Blackout Period</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">During the blackout period, directors and executive officers of the Company will be subject to the trading restrictions imposed under Section 306(a) of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002 and Regulation BTR. These restrictions generally prohibit the direct or indirect purchase, sale, or other acquisition or transfer of any equity security of the Company acquired in connection with your service as a director or employment as an executive officer of the Company. Please note that &#8220;equity securities&#8221; is defined broadly to include not only the Company&#8217;s common stock, but also stock options and other derivatives. Covered transactions are not limited to those involving your direct ownership, but also include any transaction in which you have a pecuniary interest, such as transactions by immediate family members living in your household.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Questions or Additional Information</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">If you have questions regarding this notice, the blackout period, or the restrictions described above, please contact Michael Dai, Assistant Secretary, by telephone at (651) 737-8503 or by mail at 3M Company, 3M Center, 220-10E-09, St. Paul, MN 55144.</font></div><div style="height:74.99pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div></body></html>
